@triton.jit
def triton_per_fused_convert_element_type_mean_pow_view_3(in_ptr0, out_ptr0, xnumel, r0_numel, XBLOCK : tl.constexpr):
    xnumel = 2048
    r0_numel = 512
    R0_BLOCK: tl.constexpr = 512
    rnumel = r0_numel
    RBLOCK: tl.constexpr = R0_BLOCK
    xoffset = tl.program_id(0) * XBLOCK
    xindex = xoffset + tl.arange(0, XBLOCK)[:, None]
    xmask = xindex < xnumel
    r0_index = tl.arange(0, R0_BLOCK)[None, :]
    r0_offset = 0
    r0_mask = tl.full([R0_BLOCK], True, tl.int1)[None, :]
    roffset = r0_offset
    rindex = r0_index
    r0_1 = r0_index
    x0 = xindex
    tmp0 = tl.load(in_ptr0 + (r0_1 + 512*x0), xmask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    tmp1 = tmp0.to(tl.float32)
    tmp2 = tmp1 * tmp1
    tmp3 = tl.broadcast_to(tmp2, [XBLOCK, R0_BLOCK])
    tmp5 = tl.where(xmask, tmp3, 0)
    tmp6 = tl.sum(tmp5, 1)[:, None].to(tl.float32)
    tl.store(out_ptr0 + (x0), tmp6, xmask)
''', device_str='cuda')

    arg2_1 = rand_strided((2048, 512), (512, 1), device='cuda:0', dtype=torch.bfloat16)
    arg3_1 = rand_strided((512, ), (1, ), device='cuda:0', dtype=torch.bfloat16)
    return [arg0_1, arg1_1, arg2_1, arg3_1]


def benchmark_compiled_module(args, times=10, repeat=10):
    from torch._inductor.utils import print_performance
    fn = lambda: call(list(args))
    return print_performance(fn, times=times, repeat=repeat)

@triton.jit
def triton_per_fused_convert_element_type_mean_pow_view_3(in_ptr0, out_ptr0, xnumel, r0_numel, XBLOCK : tl.constexpr):
    xnumel = 2048
    r0_numel = 512
    R0_BLOCK: tl.constexpr = 512
    rnumel = r0_numel
    RBLOCK: tl.constexpr = R0_BLOCK
    xoffset = tl.program_id(0) * XBLOCK
    xindex = xoffset + tl.arange(0, XBLOCK)[:, None]
    xmask = xindex < xnumel
    r0_index = tl.arange(0, R0_BLOCK)[None, :]
    r0_offset = 0
    r0_mask = tl.full([R0_BLOCK], True, tl.int1)[None, :]
    roffset = r0_offset
    rindex = r0_index
    r0_1 = r0_index
    x0 = xindex
    tmp0 = tl.load(in_ptr0 + (r0_1 + 512*x0), xmask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    tmp1 = tmp0.to(tl.float32)
    tmp2 = tmp1 * tmp1
    tmp3 = tl.broadcast_to(tmp2, [XBLOCK, R0_BLOCK])
    tmp5 = tl.where(xmask, tmp3, 0)
    tmp6 = tl.sum(tmp5, 1)[:, None].to(tl.float32)
    tl.store(out_ptr0 + (x0), tmp6, xmask)
''', device_str='cuda')

    arg3_1 = rand_strided((512, ), (1, ), device='cuda:0', dtype=torch.bfloat16)
    return [arg0_1, arg1_1, arg2_1, arg3_1]


def benchmark_compiled_module(args, times=10, repeat=10):
    from torch._inductor.utils import print_performance
    fn = lambda: call(list(args))
    return print_performance(fn, times=times, repeat=repeat)

@triton.jit
def triton_per_fused_convert_element_type_mean_pow_view_3(in_ptr0, out_ptr0, xnumel, r0_numel, XBLOCK : tl.constexpr):
    xnumel = 2048
    r0_numel = 512
    R0_BLOCK: tl.constexpr = 512
    rnumel = r0_numel
    RBLOCK: tl.constexpr = R0_BLOCK
    xoffset = tl.program_id(0) * XBLOCK
    xindex = xoffset + tl.arange(0, XBLOCK)[:, None]
    xmask = xindex < xnumel
    r0_index = tl.arange(0, R0_BLOCK)[None, :]
    r0_offset = 0
    r0_mask = tl.full([R0_BLOCK], True, tl.int1)[None, :]
    roffset = r0_offset
    rindex = r0_index
    r0_1 = r0_index
    x0 = xindex
    tmp0 = tl.load(in_ptr0 + (r0_1 + 512*x0), xmask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    tmp1 = tmp0.to(tl.float32)
    tmp2 = tmp1 * tmp1
    tmp3 = tl.broadcast_to(tmp2, [XBLOCK, R0_BLOCK])
    tmp5 = tl.where(xmask, tmp3, 0)
    tmp6 = tl.sum(tmp5, 1)[:, None].to(tl.float32)
    tl.store(out_ptr0 + (x0), tmp6, xmask)
''', device_str='cuda')

    from torch._inductor.utils import print_performance
    fn = lambda: call(list(args))
    return print_performance(fn, times=times, repeat=repeat)

def triton_per_fused_convert_element_type_mean_pow_view_3(in_ptr0, out_ptr0, xnumel, r0_numel, XBLOCK : tl.constexpr):
    xnumel = 2048
    r0_numel = 512
    R0_BLOCK: tl.constexpr = 512
    rnumel = r0_numel
    RBLOCK: tl.constexpr = R0_BLOCK
    xoffset = tl.program_id(0) * XBLOCK
    xindex = xoffset + tl.arange(0, XBLOCK)[:, None]
    xmask = xindex < xnumel
    r0_index = tl.arange(0, R0_BLOCK)[None, :]
    r0_offset = 0
    r0_mask = tl.full([R0_BLOCK], True, tl.int1)[None, :]
    roffset = r0_offset
    rindex = r0_index
    r0_1 = r0_index
    x0 = xindex
    tmp0 = tl.load(in_ptr0 + (r0_1 + 512*x0), xmask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    tmp1 = tmp0.to(tl.float32)
    tmp2 = tmp1 * tmp1
    tmp3 = tl.broadcast_to(tmp2, [XBLOCK, R0_BLOCK])
    tmp5 = tl.where(xmask, tmp3, 0)
    tmp6 = tl.sum(tmp5, 1)[:, None].to(tl.float32)
    tl.store(out_ptr0 + (x0), tmp6, xmask)
''', device_str='cuda')

def triton_per_fused_convert_element_type_mean_pow_view_3(in_ptr0, out_ptr0, xnumel, r0_numel, XBLOCK : tl.constexpr):

    r0_numel = 512
    R0_BLOCK: tl.constexpr = 512
    rnumel = r0_numel
    RBLOCK: tl.constexpr = R0_BLOCK
    xoffset = tl.program_id(0) * XBLOCK
    xindex = xoffset + tl.arange(0, XBLOCK)[:, None]
    xmask = xindex < xnumel
    r0_index = tl.arange(0, R0_BLOCK)[None, :]
    r0_offset = 0
    r0_mask = tl.full([R0_BLOCK], True, tl.int1)[None, :]

    rindex = r0_index
    r0_1 = r0_index
    x0 = xindex

    tmp1 = tmp0.to(tl.float32)
    tmp2 = tmp1 * tmp1
    tmp3 = tl.broadcast_to(tmp2, [XBLOCK, R0_BLOCK])
    tmp5 = tl.where(xmask, tmp3, 0)
    tmp6 = tl.sum(tmp5, 1)[:, None].to(tl.float32)
    tl.store(out_ptr0 + (x0), tmp6, xmask)
''', device_str='cuda')

def get_args():
    from torch._dynamo.testing import rand_strided
    arg0_1 = rand_strided((2048, 32768), (32768, 1), device='cuda:0', dtype=torch.bfloat16)

    arg2_1 = rand_strided((2048, 512), (512, 1), device='cuda:0', dtype=torch.bfloat16)

def benchmark_compiled_module(args, times=10, repeat=10):
    from torch._inductor.utils import print_performance
    fn = lambda: call(list(args))
    return print_performance(fn, times=times, repeat=repeat)

    args = get_args()
    compiled_module_main('None', lambda times, repeat: benchmark_compiled_module(args, times=times, repeat=repeat))

call = runner.call
recursively_apply_fns = runner.recursively_apply_fns


def get_args():
    from torch._dynamo.testing import rand_strided
    arg0_1 = rand_strided((2048, 32768), (32768, 1), device='cuda:0', dtype=torch.bfloat16)
    arg1_1 = rand_strided((32, ), (1, ), device='cuda:0', dtype=torch.bfloat16)
    arg2_1 = rand_strided((2048, 512), (512, 1), device='cuda:0', dtype=torch.bfloat16)
    arg3_1 = rand_strided((512, ), (1, ), device='cuda:0', dtype=torch.bfloat16)
    return [arg0_1, arg1_1, arg2_1, arg3_1]


def benchmark_compiled_module(args, times=10, repeat=10):
    from torch._inductor.utils import print_performance
    fn = lambda: call(list(args))
    return print_performance(fn, times=times, repeat=repeat)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    from torch._inductor.wrapper_benchmark import compiled_module_main
    args = get_args()
    compiled_module_main('None', lambda times, repeat: benchmark_compiled_module(args, times=times, repeat=repeat))
